dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSapTableExtract\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nExtracts data from an SAP table.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFilter Input\u003c/strong\u003e: Acts like a WHERE clause in SQL, allowing you to filter the table's records.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLimit Input\u003c/strong\u003e: Restricts the number of extracted records.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSapTableLoad\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nLoads data into an SAP table.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOperation Input\u003c/strong\u003e: Determines the operation to perform on the SAP system:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eINSERT: Inserts records into the table. If a record with the same primary key already exists, it will be overwritten (equivalent to a delete followed by an insert).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUPSERT: Inserts a new record if it does not exist. If the record already exists, it will be updated.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTransaction mode:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSYNC: API calls are executed sequentially.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eASYNC: API calls are executed asynchronously.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSapDelete\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nDeletes data from an SAP table based on specified keys.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSapTruncate\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eClears all data from an SAP table.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSapTableQuery\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nUsed in LU Table population to extract data from a table based on the linking field values in the parent 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDisable SSL Certificate Check\u003c/strong\u003e:\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDisables certificate validation for HTTPS connections.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChecking this parameter allows establishing a connection to a secure server using either a self-signed certificate or a certificate from an untrusted authority.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImportant\u003c/strong\u003e: While this ensures the connection is encrypted, it exposes the system to potential man-in-the-middle attacks. It is strongly recommended to address this issue by installing a certificate, which is both trusted and valid, on the server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCSRF Enabled\u003c/strong\u003e:\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSet this to \u003cstrong\u003etrue\u003c/strong\u003e if CSRF validation is enabled in the SAP system. When enabled, all API calls to SAP will utilize a CSRF token provided by SAP.\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eBehavior When Enabled:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAt the start of each SAP session, an additional API call is made to fetch the CSRF token.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf the token expires and a \u003cstrong\u003e403 CSRF validation error\u003c/strong\u003e occurs:\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe token is automatically renewed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe error is suppressed, ensuring uninterrupted API communication.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" and \"HHmmss\" (Time).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eParsed java.sql.Date and java.sql.Time objects.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSetting this flag to dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003cstrong\u003eExtract/Load\u003c/strong\u003e section of the interface includes two key parameters that impact performance:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExtract Page Size\u003c/strong\u003e:\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSpecifies the number of records to request in each API extract call.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLoad Batch Size\u003c/strong\u003e:\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDefines the number of records to load in each API load call. Note that this value may be overridden by the SapTableLoad actor.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese parameters have default values, but they can be adjusted. It is recommended to adjust the values per the table’s number of records and fields, as it would lead to a better performance. For example, when loading data in an ASYNC mode, the \u003cstrong\u003eExtract Page Size\u003c/strong\u003e parameter’s value should be higher than the \u003cstrong\u003eLoad Batch Size\u003c/strong\u003e parameter’s value.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePrefetching in as the current one is requested, ensuring it is ready for use with no delay.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003cstrong\u003eSapTableLoad\u003c/strong\u003e actor includes performance-enhancing parameters:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBatch \u0026amp; Batch Size\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSet the \u003cstrong\u003eBatch\u003c/strong\u003e to \u003cstrong\u003etrue\u003c/strong\u003e to enable loading the \u003cstrong\u003eBatch Size\u003c/strong\u003e’s number of records in each load API call.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFollowing the above setting, adjust the \u003cstrong\u003eBatch Size\u003c/strong\u003e for a better performance (the default value is set in the interface’s \u003cstrong\u003eLoad Batch Size\u003c/strong\u003e parameter).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote: If the \u003cstrong\u003eBatch\u003c/strong\u003e is set to \u003cstrong\u003etrue\u003c/strong\u003e, the stage(s) in the Broadway flow must operate in a \u003cstrong\u003eTransaction Mode\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAdditional improvement option:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo aggregate the batch records using multiple threads:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eCreate a new Broadway flow and add the \u003cstrong\u003eSapTableLoad\u003c/strong\u003e Actor -\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c6d63a242b2c6e3161a994a8bca5ba2f.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c6d63a242b2c6e3161a994a8bca5ba2f.png\" alt=\"\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn the original Load flow, call the flow created in step 1 using \u003cstrong\u003eInnerFlowAsync\u003c/strong\u003e actor.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eConfigure the number of threads by setting the \u003cstrong\u003ethreadCount\u003c/strong\u003e input in the \u003cstrong\u003eInnerFlowAsync\u003c/strong\u003e actor. The default value is 0, which allows the system to use as many threads as needed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAdd an \u003cstrong\u003eInnerFlowJoin\u003c/strong\u003e actor to the flow. Pass the \u003cstrong\u003eremaining\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003efailures\u003c/strong\u003e outputs from the \u003cstrong\u003eInnerFlowAsync\u003c/strong\u003e actor to the corresponding \u003cstrong\u003eremaining\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003efailures\u003c/strong\u003e inputs in the \u003cstrong\u003eInnerFlowJoin\u003c/strong\u003e actor. This ensures that the load flow waits for all the threads to complete before it closes.\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c8f6ab13299300c14f3d3818133e16da.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c8f6ab13299300c14f3d3818133e16da.png\" alt=\"\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTransaction Mode\u003c/strong\u003e: Controls how API calls are made:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSYNC\u003c/strong\u003e: API calls are executed sequentially.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eASYNC\u003c/strong\u003e: API calls are executed asynchronously. During the commit process, the interface ensures that all API calls are successfully completed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRemoved TDMSourceDbQuery dependency in SapTableQuery actor which caused a compilation error.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFixed an issue in SapTableLoad of case-sensitivity in the fields names that caused a SapApiException (\"Expected the same amount of fields and values\"). This happenned when an item in \u003ccode\u003efields\u003c/code\u003e param did not exactly match a key of \u003ccode\u003eparams\u003c/code\u003e map.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAdded an empty batch check in \u003ccode\u003eSapTableLoad\u003c/code\u003e \u003ccode\u003ecommit\u003c/code\u003e method to avoid calling the API without any data. This caused an API failure when there's nothing to commit in the last batch.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eResolved an issue causing unnecessary extract API calls when closing an inner flow that returns a \u003ccode\u003eSapExtractResult\u003c/code\u003e, by ensuring the same iterator is always returned instead of creating a new one each time.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePreviously, when a field of type \u003ccode\u003enumber\u003c/code\u003e was empty, it was incorrectly converted to \u003ccode\u003e0\u003c/code\u003e instead of \u003ccode\u003enull\u003c/code\u003e. This caused issues when the data was reloaded into the same table, as the SAP API failed because \u003ccode\u003e0\u003c/code\u003e is not a valid timestamp (apparently that specific field represented a timestamp in SAP).\nA check has now been added to correctly handle empty values by returning \u003ccode\u003enull\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eAdded\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-added\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Added\" href=\"#added\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eNew actor \u003ccode\u003eSapTruncate\u003c/code\u003e that can truncate a SAP table.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMultithreading support for batch loading.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIntroduced several new inputs for SapTableLoad actor:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eoperation\u003c/code\u003e - Allows selection between \u003ccode\u003eINSERT\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eUPSERT\u003c/code\u003e. itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SAP Connector</h1><a id="user-content-sap-connector" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SAP Connector" href="#sap-connector"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 <h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Introduction</h1><a id="user-content-introduction" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Introduction" href="#introduction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The SAP Connector library is designed to enable seamless integration between K2view and SAP systems.</p>
<p dir="auto">The connector uses APIs specifically built for the K2view connector, which must be installed on the SAP system.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SAP Broadway Actors</h2><a id="user-content-sap-broadway-actors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SAP Broadway Actors" href="#sap-broadway-actors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The library includes five built-in Actors:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>SapTableExtract</strong><br>
Extracts data from an SAP table.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Filter Input</strong>: Acts like a WHERE clause in SQL, allowing you to filter the table's records.</li>
<li><strong>Limit Input</strong>: Restricts the number of extracted records.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>SapTableLoad</strong><br>
Loads data into an SAP table.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Operation Input</strong>: Determines the operation to perform on the SAP system:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>INSERT: Inserts records into the table. If a record with the same primary key already exists, it will be overwritten (equivalent to a delete followed by an insert).</li>
<li>UPSERT: Inserts a new record if it does not exist. If the record already exists, it will be updated.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Transaction mode:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>SYNC: API calls are executed sequentially.</li>
<li>ASYNC: API calls are executed asynchronously.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>SapDelete</strong><br>
Deletes data from an SAP table based on specified keys.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>SapTruncate</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Clears all data from an SAP table.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>SapTableQuery</strong><br>
Used in LU Table population to extract data from a table based on the linking field values in the parent table.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SAP LU Tables</h2><a id="user-content-sap-lu-tables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SAP LU Tables" href="#sap-lu-tables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add tables to the LU Schema, use the <strong>DB Explorer</strong>. After running the <strong>Catalog</strong> on the SAP interface, the DB Explorer will display the available tables.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h1><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Requirements</h2><a id="user-content-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Requirements" href="#requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<h4 dir="auto"></h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Fabric Version</strong>: 8.1.0 or higher</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Install the SAP Connector</h2><a id="user-content-step-1-install-the-sap-connector" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Install the SAP Connector" href="#step-1-install-the-sap-connector"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Open your Studio and navigate to the <strong>Extensions</strong> section.</li>
<li>Locate the <strong>SAP Connector</strong> extension in the list.</li>
<li>Click <strong>Install</strong> to add it to your project.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/e1d4a17bd0258cd5814b6065afb3f407.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/e1d4a17bd0258cd5814b6065afb3f407.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2: Install SAP TR Files on Your SAP System</h2><a id="user-content-step-2-install-sap-tr-files-on-your-sap-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2: Install SAP TR Files on Your SAP System" href="#step-2-install-sap-tr-files-on-your-sap-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the Studio, navigate to <strong>Project → Project Resources → SAP → TRs</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Download the appropriate zip file based on your SAP system and namespace:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ECC-Z</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ECC-ZY</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>S4HANA-Z</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/78953fd0b10bc3a177339c0aa293c031.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/78953fd0b10bc3a177339c0aa293c031.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Install the file on your SAP system.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3: Validate SAP System Installation</h2><a id="user-content-step-3-validate-sap-system-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3: Validate SAP System Installation" href="#step-3-validate-sap-system-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Refer to the instructions in the <strong>Sanity Check Document - Post TR Import-v2.pdf</strong> document to ensure a proper installation of the SAP system.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 4: Create and Validate SAP DB Interface</h2><a id="user-content-step-4-create-and-validate-sap-db-interface" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 4: Create and Validate SAP DB Interface" href="#step-4-create-and-validate-sap-db-interface"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Create an SAP Interface</h3><a id="user-content-create-an-sap-interface" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Create an SAP Interface" href="#create-an-sap-interface"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>In the <strong>Studio</strong>, navigate to <strong>Project → Implementation → Shared Objects → Interfaces</strong>.</li>
<li>Right-click on <strong>Interfaces</strong> and select <strong>New Interface</strong> -<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/fd8faeb907b0074f136df8c6fd18d8bf.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/fd8faeb907b0074f136df8c6fd18d8bf.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
<li>Choose <strong>SAP</strong> as the Interface Type -<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/4a907694a67dcd56ca731b472a2b7012.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/4a907694a67dcd56ca731b472a2b7012.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
<li>Name the new interface -<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/984aab221fbcead533db80633f190054.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/984aab221fbcead533db80633f190054.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
<li>Enter the connection details for the SAP system (refer to the below <em>Mandatory Parameters for Interface Creation</em> section).</li>
<li>Save the interface configuration.</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"></h3>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mandatory Parameters for Interface Creation</h3><a id="user-content-mandatory-parameters-for-interface-creation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mandatory Parameters for Interface Creation" href="#mandatory-parameters-for-interface-creation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Connection Parameters:</strong></h4><a id="user-content-connection-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Connection Parameters:" href="#connection-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Protocol Type</strong>: HTTP/HTTPS</li>
<li><strong>Host</strong>: SAP system host</li>
<li><strong>Port</strong>: SAP system port</li>
<li><strong>User</strong>: Username for connecting to the SAP system</li>
<li><strong>Password</strong>: Password for the SAP system</li>
<li><strong>SAP Namespace</strong>: SAP namespace</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Security Parameters:</strong></h4><a id="user-content-security-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security Parameters:" href="#security-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Disable SSL Certificate Check</strong>:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Disables certificate validation for HTTPS connections.</li>
<li>Checking this parameter allows establishing a connection to a secure server using either a self-signed certificate or a certificate from an untrusted authority.</li>
<li><strong>Important</strong>: While this ensures the connection is encrypted, it exposes the system to potential man-in-the-middle attacks. It is strongly recommended to address this issue by installing a certificate, which is both trusted and valid, on the server.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>CSRF Enabled</strong>:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Set this to <strong>true</strong> if CSRF validation is enabled in the SAP system. When enabled, all API calls to SAP will utilize a CSRF token provided by SAP.<br>
<strong>Behavior When Enabled:</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>At the start of each SAP session, an additional API call is made to fetch the CSRF token.</li>
<li>If the token expires and a <strong>403 CSRF validation error</strong> occurs:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>The token is automatically renewed.</li>
<li>The error is suppressed, ensuring uninterrupted API communication.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Optional Parameters for Debugging and Data Handling:</strong></h4><a id="user-content-optional-parameters-for-debugging-and-data-handling" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Optional Parameters for Debugging and Data Handling:" href="#optional-parameters-for-debugging-and-data-handling"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Debug Logging</strong>:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>When set to <strong>true</strong>, it logs each SAP API call at the INFO level, including the API path, payload and response.</li>
<li>For more detailed debugging:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Leave this flag off.</li>
<li>Configure logback.xml to show DEBUG-level logs from com.k2view.cdbms.usercode.common.sap for more granular information.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>Use String for Date/Time</strong>:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>SAP Date and Time values can be retrieved as either one of these two options:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Strings in the format "YYYYmmdd" (Date) and "HHmmss" (Time).</li>
<li>Parsed java.sql.Date and java.sql.Time objects.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Setting this flag to <strong>true</strong> retains the values as strings.</li>
<li><strong>Recommendation</strong>: Enable this flag unless specific database formatting or Date/Time parsing is explicitly required. Enabling this flag would prevent inconsistencies across systems.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Optimization Parameters (Extract/Load):</strong></h4><a id="user-content-optimization-parameters-extractload" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Optimization Parameters (Extract/Load):" href="#optimization-parameters-extractload"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Extract Page Size</strong>: Specifies the number of records to fetch in each Extract API call.</li>
<li><strong>Load Batch Size</strong>: Defines the number of records to upload in each Load API call.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Validate the Interface</h3><a id="user-content-validate-the-interface" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Validate the Interface" href="#validate-the-interface"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In the interface, click <strong>Test Connection</strong> to ensure the connection is functioning as expected.</p>
<p dir="auto">Testing the connection verifies the connectivity between Fabric and the SAP system, ensuring successful integration.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How To Use</h1><a id="user-content-how-to-use" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How To Use" href="#how-to-use"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Create Catalog for your SAP Tables</h2><a id="user-content-step-1-create-catalog-for-your-sap-tables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Create Catalog for your SAP Tables" href="#step-1-create-catalog-for-your-sap-tables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Navigate to: <strong>Project → Implementation → Shared Objects → Interfaces → Discovery</strong> in Studio.</li>
<li>Open the plugins.discovery file.
<ol dir="auto">
<li>In the data_platforms section, add an entry for the SAP interface, specifying the SAP tables to include in the Data Discovery.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Save the file by pressing <strong>Ctrl + S</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Important Notes:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">SAP systems contain many tables. It is mandatory to specify the required tables in the data_platform section in order to avoid processing all tables. This section should not be left empty.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <strong>Category</strong> property of SAP tables serves as the tables’ schema.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The tables listed in the data_platform must include the schema name (Category). If the Category is unknown, use "*" as a wildcard to represent the schema.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/1b7f74870716df07560d841f565e8c06.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/1b7f74870716df07560d841f565e8c06.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2: Run the Catalog’s discovery process</h2><a id="user-content-step-2-run-the-catalogs-discovery-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2: Run the Catalog’s discovery process" href="#step-2-run-the-catalogs-discovery-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<h4 dir="auto"></h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to <strong>Project → Implementation → Shared Objects → Interfaces → Other</strong> in your studio.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Right-click the SAP interface you intend to run the Catalog on and select 'Run Discovery Job' -</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/23e49f03da8f0f2dca14ee24c900bbe6.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/23e49f03da8f0f2dca14ee24c900bbe6.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Validate that the Discovery Job has finished, and a new Catalog was created. Expect to see the below pop-up window:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/650fecb76daea03cbdb44b0e0f66ead2.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/650fecb76daea03cbdb44b0e0f66ead2.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Open the Catalog to see the created relations -<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/8676d7f88759b4f4836cd94262ed1138.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/8676d7f88759b4f4836cd94262ed1138.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Build the artifacts for the newly generated Catalog -</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/1a803e8f748d68d76bdb996a3502a757.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/1a803e8f748d68d76bdb996a3502a757.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3: Add SAP Tables to your LU Schema</h2><a id="user-content-step-3-add-sap-tables-to-your-lu-schema" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3: Add SAP Tables to your LU Schema" href="#step-3-add-sap-tables-to-your-lu-schema"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Create a New LU Schema</h4><a id="user-content-create-a-new-lu-schema" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Create a New LU Schema" href="#create-a-new-lu-schema"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Navigate to: <strong>Project → Implementation</strong>.
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Right-click on <strong>Logical Units/Data Product</strong> and select ‘<strong>New Data Product (Logical Unit)...’</strong>.</li>
<li>Name the new Logical Unit (LU) and select the default type.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Add SAP Tables to the LU Schema</h4><a id="user-content-add-sap-tables-to-the-lu-schema" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Add SAP Tables to the LU Schema" href="#add-sap-tables-to-the-lu-schema"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Open the schema of the newly created LU.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Go to the <strong>INTERFACE EXPLORER</strong> tab.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Open the <strong>SAP Interface</strong> and locate the root table.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Right-click on the root table and select <strong>Add Table to Schema with Descendants</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/031fdf1785a5761aa0893195fe55ca36.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/031fdf1785a5761aa0893195fe55ca36.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">This action will include the root table along with its related tables in the schema.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/78e729b4fa23d475eebb28c6523dc0a4.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/78e729b4fa23d475eebb28c6523dc0a4.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance considerations</h1><a id="user-content-performance-considerations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance considerations" href="#performance-considerations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Interface Parameters</h2><a id="user-content-interface-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Interface Parameters" href="#interface-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <strong>Extract/Load</strong> section of the interface includes two key parameters that impact performance:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Extract Page Size</strong>:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Specifies the number of records to request in each API extract call.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>Load Batch Size</strong>:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Defines the number of records to load in each API load call. Note that this value may be overridden by the SapTableLoad actor.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">These parameters have default values, but they can be adjusted. It is recommended to adjust the values per the table’s number of records and fields, as it would lead to a better performance. For example, when loading data in an ASYNC mode, the <strong>Extract Page Size</strong> parameter’s value should be higher than the <strong>Load Batch Size</strong> parameter’s value.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prefetching in Extract Actors</h3><a id="user-content-prefetching-in-extract-actors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prefetching in Extract Actors" href="#prefetching-in-extract-actors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">As SAP data is retrieved in pages, a mechanism was added to prefetch the subsequent page as soon as the current one is requested, ensuring it is ready for use with no delay.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Broadway Actor Parameters</h2><a id="user-content-broadway-actor-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Broadway Actor Parameters" href="#broadway-actor-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <strong>SapTableLoad</strong> actor includes performance-enhancing parameters:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Batch &amp; Batch Size</strong>:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Set the <strong>Batch</strong> to <strong>true</strong> to enable loading the <strong>Batch Size</strong>’s number of records in each load API call.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Following the above setting, adjust the <strong>Batch Size</strong> for a better performance (the default value is set in the interface’s <strong>Load Batch Size</strong> parameter).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Note: If the <strong>Batch</strong> is set to <strong>true</strong>, the stage(s) in the Broadway flow must operate in a <strong>Transaction Mode</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Additional improvement option:</p>
<p dir="auto">To aggregate the batch records using multiple threads:</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Create a new Broadway flow and add the <strong>SapTableLoad</strong> Actor -</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c6d63a242b2c6e3161a994a8bca5ba2f.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c6d63a242b2c6e3161a994a8bca5ba2f.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the original Load flow, call the flow created in step 1 using <strong>InnerFlowAsync</strong> actor.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Configure the number of threads by setting the <strong>threadCount</strong> input in the <strong>InnerFlowAsync</strong> actor. The default value is 0, which allows the system to use as many threads as needed.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Add an <strong>InnerFlowJoin</strong> actor to the flow. Pass the <strong>remaining</strong> and <strong>failures</strong> outputs from the <strong>InnerFlowAsync</strong> actor to the corresponding <strong>remaining</strong> and <strong>failures</strong> inputs in the <strong>InnerFlowJoin</strong> actor. This ensures that the load flow waits for all the threads to complete before it closes.<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/blob/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c8f6ab13299300c14f3d3818133e16da.png"><img src="/k2view-COE-KB/SAP/raw/sap-core-8.1/extensions/sap-connector/media/c8f6ab13299300c14f3d3818133e16da.png" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Transaction Mode</strong>: Controls how API calls are made:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>SYNC</strong>: API calls are executed sequentially.</li>
<li><strong>ASYNC</strong>: API calls are executed asynchronously. During the commit process, the interface ensures that all API calls are successfully completed.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>INSERT Mode</strong>:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>When using <strong>SapTableLoad</strong>, choose <strong>INSERT Mode</strong> whenever possible, for better performance.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changelog</h1><a id="user-content-changelog" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changelog" href="#changelog"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v1.0.1</h2><a id="user-content-v101" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v1.0.1" href="#v101"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fixed</h3><a id="user-content-fixed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fixed" href="#fixed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Resolved an occasional ConcurrentModificationException that occurred during the transition to the next page while cleaning up the current page.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed</h3><a id="user-content-changed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed" href="#changed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The CSRF token is now stored for each SAP system host instead of each SapConnection, reducing unnecessary CSRF token fetches.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v1.0.0</h2><a id="user-content-v100" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v1.0.0" href="#v100"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fixed</h3><a id="user-content-fixed-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fixed" href="#fixed-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Removed TDMSourceDbQuery dependency in SapTableQuery actor which caused a compilation error.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue in SapTableLoad of case-sensitivity in the fields names that caused a SapApiException ("Expected the same amount of fields and values"). This happenned when an item in <code>fields</code> param did not exactly match a key of <code>params</code> map.</li>
<li>Added an empty batch check in <code>SapTableLoad</code> <code>commit</code> method to avoid calling the API without any data. This caused an API failure when there's nothing to commit in the last batch.</li>
<li>Resolved an issue causing unnecessary extract API calls when closing an inner flow that returns a <code>SapExtractResult</code>, by ensuring the same iterator is always returned instead of creating a new one each time.</li>
<li>Previously, when a field of type <code>number</code> was empty, it was incorrectly converted to <code>0</code> instead of <code>null</code>. This caused issues when the data was reloaded into the same table, as the SAP API failed because <code>0</code> is not a valid timestamp (apparently that specific field represented a timestamp in SAP).
A check has now been added to correctly handle empty values by returning <code>null</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Added</h3><a id="user-content-added" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Added" href="#added"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>New actor <code>SapTruncate</code> that can truncate a SAP table.</li>
<li>Multithreading support for batch loading.</li>
<li>Introduced several new inputs for SapTableLoad actor:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>operation</code> - Allows selection between <code>INSERT</code> and <code>UPSERT</code>. Previously, the only supported operation was <code>UPSERT</code>. The <code>INSERT</code> option, which is functionally similar to performing a delete followed by an insert, offers improved performance compared to <code>UPSERT</code>.</li>
<li><code>transactionMode</code> - accepts one of two predefined values: <code>SYNC</code> for synchronous execution, where batch-load APIs are executed one at a time, or <code>ASYNC</code> for asynchronous execution, enabling concurrent batch-load API executions.</li>
<li><code>maxConcurrentApiCalls</code> (default: 20) applies only in <code>ASYNC</code> mode. When the limit is reached, the oldest API call must finish before submitting a new batch.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Added support for CSRF validation - can be turned on/off in the interface settings.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed</h3><a id="user-content-changed-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed" href="#changed-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Updated the fetching logic in the extraction process to prefetch the next page asynchronously immediately after fetching the current page, ensuring no delay when the next page is requested.</li>
<li>Refactoring and minor performance enhancements in SapTableLoad actor.</li>
<li>Values of <code>params</code> in SapTableLoad actor now take precedence over additional actor inputs.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v0.0.9</h2><a id="user-content-v009" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v0.0.9" href="#v009"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v0.0.8</h2><a id="user-content-v008" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v0.0.8" href="#v008"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fixed</h3><a id="user-content-fixed-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fixed" href="#fixed-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Changed catalog field property "Decimal Precision" to "decimalPrecision" following a discovery job failure in Fabric Studio: 8.1.0-14, Fabric: 8.1.1_12.</li>
<li>Changed the sqlite and catalog data type mapping for date and time to VARCHAR when the flag "Use String for Date/Time" is set. This changes the type of Date/Time fields to TEXT in the LU tables which are created automatically based on the Catalog, as it was failing in the population when trying to insert a string into a Date or Time field.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v0.0.6</h2><a id="user-content-v006" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v0.0.6" href="#v006"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Added</h3><a id="user-content-added-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Added" href="#added-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A flag in the SAP interface which provides the ability to treat SAP dates and times as either a string or a java.sql.Date/Time</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fixed</h3><a id="user-content-fixed-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fixed" href="#fixed-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Overriding fetch size in the extract actor - was taking it always from the interface.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v0.0.5</h2><a id="user-content-v005" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v0.0.5" href="#v005"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fixed</h3><a id="user-content-fixed-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fixed" href="#fixed-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
